"result": {
"task_id": "SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID"}}`

## [tag/AI-Hair-Extension/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-ext/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Extension/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-ext/get) Check the status of a AI Hair Extension task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-ext

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-ext

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Hair Extension task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

### Request samples

- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

    --url 'https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-ext?task_id=SX9ALF1Z%2BKIiNa%2BGaFRp4bI5gijoc%2FckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc%2B%2B3iXXdKqnU4%2FLID' \
    --header 'Authorization: Bearer <access_token>'

## [tag/AI-Hair-Bang-Generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Bang-Generator) AI Hair Bang Generator

### AI Hair Bang Generator

Try on Your Perfect Hair Bangs with AI
Realistic Looks: Experiment with realistic bangs and discover the style that best complements your face.​
Versatile Styling Options: Explore a wide range of bangs styles to suit every personality and occasion.​
Effortless Experience: Enjoy a user-friendly interface that makes trying new bangs easy and fun​.

Want to see more Hair Bang styles? Please refer to [https://yce.perfectcorp.com/bangs-filter](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/bangs-filter).

Use case:

![AI Hair Bang Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/hair_style_v1_video_1200x674px_1_259f619dfd.png)

![AI Hair Bang Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/hair_style_v1_video_1200x674px_2_7146754733.png)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Hair Bang Generator | long side <= 1024, face width >= 128, face pose: -10 < pitch < +10, -45 < yaw < +45, -15 < roll < +15, single face only, need to show full face | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg/png |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_no\_shoulder | Shoulders are not visible in the source image |
| error\_large\_face\_angle | The face angle in the uploaded image is too large |
| error\_insufficient\_landmarks | Cannot detect sufficient face or body landmarks in the source image |
| error\_hair\_too\_short | Input hair is too short |
| error\_face\_pose | The face pose of source image is unsupported |
| error\_bald\_image | Input hairstyle is bald |

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

## [tag/AI-Hair-Bang-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-bang/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Bang-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-bang/post) Run a AI Hair Bang Generator task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-bang

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-bang

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. | | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply hair bang generator. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Hair Bang Generator task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

- curl

## [tag/AI-Hair-Bang-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-bang/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Bang-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-bang/get) Check the status of a AI Hair Bang Generator task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-bang

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-bang

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Hair Bang Generator task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator) AI Hair Volume Generator

### AI Hair Volume Generator

Enhance Your Look with Fuller, More Voluminous Hair Instantly!​
Add natural volume to fine or thinning hair. Seamlessly fill gaps or add hair with AI. Works for all hair types: straight, curly, thin. Perfect for dating profiles, resumes & more.
Our AI tool helps you achieve perfect hair volume and density in all your photos, whether for personal, professional, or social use. Say goodbye to bad hair days in pictures and hello to fresh, voluminous hair every time.

Use case:
![AI Hair Volume Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/YCE_web_Hair_Volume_Filter_S4_img_01_836436ca00.jpg)

![AI Hair Volume Generator](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2024-08-26/51eadc51-aaa7-4ebc-ac78-e389be5e16b0.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Hair Volume Generator | long side <= 1024, face width >= 128, face pose: -10 < pitch < +10, -45 < yaw < +45, -15 < roll < +15, single face only, need to show full face | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg/png |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_no\_shoulder | Shoulders are not visible in the source image |
| error\_large\_face\_angle | The face angle in the uploaded image is too large |
| error\_insufficient\_landmarks | Cannot detect sufficient face or body landmarks in the source image |
| error\_hair\_too\_short | Input hair is too short |
| error\_face\_pose | The face pose of source image is unsupported |
| error\_bald\_image | Input hairstyle is bald |

## [tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1file~1hair-vol/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1file~1hair-vol/post) Create a new file.

post/s2s/v1.1/file/hair-vol

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/file/hair-vol

To upload a new file, you'll first need to use the File API. It will give you a URL – use that URL to upload your file. Once the upload is finished, you can use the file\_id from the same response to start using our AI features.

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| files<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| content\_type<br>required | string<br>Enum:"image/jpg""image/jpeg""image/png"<br>Content MIME type for this file. Currently available values are listed in the enum. |
| file\_name<br>required | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_size<br>required | integer<br>Content length for this file in bytes. Should not be larger than 10MB. | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of file upload information

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| files | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| content\_type | string<br>Content MIME type for this file. |
| file\_name | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_id | string<br>ID of this file. Other run task API will need this `file_id`. |
| requests | Array of objects<br>Using upload `url`, `headers`, `method` below to upload file. After completion, the `file_id` is used to proceed with calling run task API. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| headers | object<br>Headers to include when uploading the file |
| url | string<br>URL to upload this file |
| method | string<br>HTTP method to upload this file | | | |

Invalid request parameters

## [tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1hair-vol/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1hair-vol/get) List predefined style by category

get/s2s/v1.1/task/style/hair-vol

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/hair-vol

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of category and its styles

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |

| results | Array of objects (Category) |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of category. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of category. |
| styles<br>required | Array of objects (Style) <br>The styles belong to this category. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style group. Use this as `style_group_id` when run task. |
| style\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style. Use this as `style_ids` when run task. |
| info<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| title<br>required | string<br>The style name |
| thumb<br>required | string<br>The thumbnail of style | | |
| sub\_categories<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of sub-category. Use this id to query for its content. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of sub-category. | | |

## [tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-vol/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-vol/post) Run a AI Hair Volume Generator task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-vol

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-vol

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. | | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply hair volume generator. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Hair Volume Generator task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

## [tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-vol/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Hair-Volume-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-vol/get) Check the status of a AI Hair Volume Generator task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-vol

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-vol

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Hair Volume Generator task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Wavy-Hair](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Wavy-Hair) AI Wavy Hair

### AI Wavy Hair

Whether you're dreaming of bouncy ringlets, loose waves, or a bold curly statement, the YouCam Online Editor’s curly hair filter lets you experiment with a fresh, fabulous hairstyle in seconds—all from the comfort of home.

Whether you’re testing a soft wave or a wild afro, YouCam delivers precision and realism that other tools can’t match. It’s perfect for anyone wanting to experiment nobel hairstyle risk-free and make people look forward to their next salon visit.

![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2025-04-01/webp_03963789-fb1e-4ad8-be4d-48932e247376.jpg)

![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2025-03-20/b25b228a-259b-4efb-a7c1-31d200b62e8c.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Wavy Hair | long side <= 1024, face width >= 128, face pose: -10 < pitch < +10, -45 < yaw < +45, -15 < roll < +15, single face only, need to show full face | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg/png |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_no\_shoulder | Shoulders are not visible in the source image |
| error\_large\_face\_angle | The face angle in the uploaded image is too large |
| error\_insufficient\_landmarks | Cannot detect sufficient face or body landmarks in the source image |
| error\_hair\_too\_short | Input hair is too short |
| error\_face\_pose | The face pose of source image is unsupported |

## [tag/AI-Wavy-Hair/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-curl/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Wavy-Hair/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-curl/post) Run a AI Wavy Hair task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-curl

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-curl

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. | | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply hair wavy generator. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Wavy Hair task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

## [tag/AI-Wavy-Hair/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-curl/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Wavy-Hair/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1hair-curl/get) Check the status of a AI Wavy Hair task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-curl

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/hair-curl

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Wavy Hair task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Clothes](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Clothes) AI Clothes

### AI Clothes

AI Clothes is a virtual fitting room that lets users try on clothes without physically wearing them. Using AI and photo editing technology, these apps overlay outfits onto your image so you can see how different styles and fits look on your body type. It’s perfect for online shopping, style inspiration, or just playing around with fashion ideas. Try on clothes virtually with AI Clothes . Upload any clothing reference to swap outfits with you photo for an instant virtual wardrobe transformation.

#### How to Change Clothes in Photos with AI

- Upload Your Photo

Upload a full body photo of yourself. The virtual outfit changer works best with high resolution photos that show your clothes clearly. The photo background should not have too many people or distracting objects.


#### Try-On Predefined Styles

- There are two ways to list outfits for AI Clothes virtual try-on:
  - _**v1.0/task/style-group/cloth**_ and _**v1.0/task/style/cloth**_: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group.
  - _**v1.1/task/style/cloth**_: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again.

#### For Custom Clothing Virtual Try-On

- Using the _**v1.1/file/cloth**_ API, please upload the following assets:

  - A reference image of the clothing
  - A full-body photo to serve as the virtual try-on target
- Execute AI task _**v1.0/task/cloth**_ with the clothing image file\_id as ref\_ids and the target user image file\_id as src\_ids.

- To ensure the best results, please follow these requirements:

  - Image Requirements

    - For both the reference clothing image and the target user image, a resolution of 1024×768 is recommended (minimum 512×384).
    - The person should occupy at least 80% of the frame for optimal results.
  - Match Clothing Type to Selected Body Area

    - When selecting Upper Body, the garment must be a top.
    - When selecting Lower Body, the garment must be pants or a skirt.
    - For Dresses or Full-Body Outfits, select Full Body—not upper or lower body individually.
  - Target User Image Requirements

    - The image must show the abdomen to face, including shoulders.
    - The face must be fully visible, with no obstructions.
    - The body must be facing forward in a standing position (no sitting or crouching).
  - If Using a Real-Person Clothing Photo as Reference

    - Must feature only one person.
    - The visible clothing area must fully cover the intended try-on area.
      - Example: For full-body try-on, a half-body clothing image is not acceptable.
      - Example: For lower-body try-on, partial pants are not acceptable.
    - The clothing must not be heavily obstructed (e.g. covered by long hair or arms).
    - The image must show abdomen to face and shoulders, with the subject facing forward and standing upright.
  - If Using a Product Image as Reference

    - Must be a front-facing product shot of a single garment.
    - Do not use composite images (e.g. top and bottom in one photo).
  - Unsupported Clothing Types

    - Garments with minimal coverage, such as bikinis or underwear, are not currently supported.

> **Warning:** Note on Try-On Region Conflicts
> If there's a mismatch between the selected try-on region and the uploaded clothing image, the system will default to the region defined by the clothing image.
> Example: If you select "Full Body" but upload an upper-body-only garment, only the upper body will be applied.

> **Warning:** You need to ensure that your source image includes the necessary body part for the virtual clothing to be applied; otherwise, an _**error\_apply\_region\_mismatch**_ error will be triggered.

> **Warning:** If the chosen clothing style doesn’t match the body area selected for application, the system prioritizes the clothing image to determine where it will be applied. For example, if a user chooses to apply clothing to the whole body but uploads an image of only the upper body, the clothing will be applied only to the upper body.

Use cases:
![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2025-05-08/b80f4ae1-c905-4ec0-b491-e42c15e65575.gif)

![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/strapi/assets/01%20ai%20clothes%20changer.jpg)

![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2023-12-01/45f451aa-4b4f-466d-9da7-4538573c92af.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/strapi/assets/AI-Cloth-Guideline.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Clothes | long side <= 4096, single person only, The abdomen, face, and shoulders should all be visible. The face must not be obstructed. The body should be upright and facing forward, without any unusual poses like sitting or squatting. | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_invalid\_ref | The uploaded clothing image appears empty or only partially visible |
| error\_apply\_region\_mismatch | The source and reference images don’t match — for example, the source image shows only the upper body, while the reference image is focused on pants |
| invalid\_parameter | \- Invalid garment category <br> \- Style\_id not in inference\_style\_list <br> \- Invalid keys/acts |
| error\_download\_image | \- Download image error |
| exceed\_max\_filesize | \- image size too large (> 10MB) |
| error\_nsfw\_content\_detected | \- Potential NSFW content detected in result image |
| unknown\_internal\_error | \- Failed to load model <br> \- Invalid scheduler algorithm type <br> \- No engine loaded <br> \- File not in the upload results |

## [tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1file~1cloth/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1file~1cloth/post) Create a new file.

## [tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1cloth/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1cloth/get) List predefined style by category

get/s2s/v1.1/task/style/cloth

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/cloth

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

## [tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1cloth/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1cloth/post) Run an Clothes task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/cloth

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/cloth

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API |
| ref\_ids | Array of strings<br>ID of the reference image. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id | integer<br>Id of style group. It's required if reference image did not provide. |
| style\_ids | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. It's required if reference image did not provide. |
| garment\_category | string<br>Enum:"full\_body""lower\_body""upper\_body"<br>The category of garement of reference image. It's required if reference image provided. | | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the Clothes task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

"actions": [\
{\
"id": 0,\

## [tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1cloth/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Clothes/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1cloth/get) Check the status of the Clothes task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/cloth

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/cloth

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the Clothes task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Fabric](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Fabric) AI Fabric

### AI Fabric

Transform your look with stunning realism! Explore unique fabric styles with photo mode — whether it's the elegance of silky textures or the vibrance of bold prints, the AI Fabric API brings materials to life! Developers can craft immersive experiences that let users see and feel fabrics like never before. Plus, fresh fabric updates are always on the way!

#### How to Change Cloth Fabric Styles in Photos with AI

- Upload Your Photo

Upload a full body photo of yourself. The virtual outfit changer works best with high resolution photos that show your clothes clearly. The photo background should not have too many people or distracting objects.

- There are two ways to list outfits for AI Fabric virtual try-on:

  - v1.0: First, call the style-group to retrieve groups, then call the style to access styles within the group you're interested in.
  - v1.1: Call the predefined style list by category without passing a category\_id. Categories will include either styles or subcategories — if there’s only one layer, categories will only contain styles. If there are multiple layers, they’ll have subcategories. If you want to explore a subcategory, pass its ID in category\_id and call again.

> **Warning:** You need to ensure that your source image includes the necessary body part for the virtual clothing to be applied; otherwise, an _**error\_apply\_region\_not\_detected**_ error will be triggered.

Use cases:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/strapi/assets/AI%20Fabric.png)

![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2024-05-07/b103976d-1b0e-4bed-aab4-9307308b84d7.jpg)

![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/strapi/assets/03%20ai%20clothes%20changer.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/strapi/assets/AI-Cloth-Guideline.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Fabric | long side <= 4096, single person only, The abdomen, face, and shoulders should all be visible. The face must not be obstructed. The body should be upright and facing forward, without any unusual poses like sitting or squatting. | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_apply\_region\_not\_detected | The clothing area is either too small or wasn’t detected in the input image |

## [tag/AI-Fabric/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1file~1fabric/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Fabric/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1file~1fabric/post) Create a new file.

post/s2s/v1.1/file/fabric

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/file/fabric

To upload a new file, you'll first need to use the File API. It will give you a URL – use that URL to upload your file. Once the upload is finished, you can use the file\_id from the same response to start using our AI features.

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| files<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

| file\_name<br>required | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_size<br>required | integer<br>Content length for this file in bytes. Should not be larger than 10MB. | |

### Responses

Successful retrieval of file upload information

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

| --- | --- |

| Array

|     |     |

| content\_type | string<br>Content MIME type for this file. |
| file\_name | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_id | string<br>ID of this file. Other run task API will need this `file_id`. |
| requests | Array of objects<br>Using upload `url`, `headers`, `method` below to upload file. After completion, the `file_id` is used to proceed with calling run task API. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| headers | object<br>Headers to include when uploading the file |
| url | string<br>URL to upload this file |
| method | string<br>HTTP method to upload this file | | | |

## [tag/AI-Fabric/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1fabric/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Fabric/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1fabric/post) Run an Fabric task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/fabric

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/fabric

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. | | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the Fabric task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- curl

## [tag/AI-Fabric/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1fabric/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Fabric/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1fabric/get) Check the status of the Fabric task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/fabric

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/fabric

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the Fabric task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Object-Removal](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Object-Removal) AI Object Removal

### AI Object Removal

Remove unwanted objects with precision from your photos while preserving intricate details.
To use this amazing feature, simply input a photo along with a grayscale mask where white pixels indicate foreground elements and black pixels represent background areas. The AI Object Removal then leverages advanced algorithms to produce natural-looking images by effectively removing unwanted objects such as people, reflections, shadows, and other distractions from your photos.

## [tag/AI-Photo-Enhance](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Enhance) AI Photo Enhance

### AI Photo Enhance

AI Photo Enhancer uses advanced AI and deep learning to analyze image details and improve resolution, making low-resolution images clear & fix motion blur.

- No More Pixelation: Eliminate pixelation for smoother, more defined images.
- Fix Blurry Photos: Remove blurriness to reveal sharper, crisper details.
- Enhance Quality: Bring out finer details, making every part of your image stand out.
- Sharpen Images: Increase sharpness for clearer and more vivid images.
- Improve Clarity: Boost overall clarity to make your photos look fresh and professional.
- Face Enhancement: Refine facial features for more lifelike, enhanced portraits in motional images.

## [tag/AI-Photo-Enhance/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1enhance/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Enhance/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1enhance/post) Run an AI Photo Enhance task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/enhance

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/enhance

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to run enhancement. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| scale<br>required | integer<br>Scaling ratio. Available values are 1, 2, 4. | | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Photo Enhance task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- Payload
- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

Content type

"payload": {

"src_ids": [\
"pfNK5PuRe0MrwLHcGA3DOmB1ahwfXTbYHjv+KoBIxbE="]},
"actions": [\
{\
"id": 0,\
"params": {\
"scale": 1}}]}}`

## [tag/AI-Photo-Enhance/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1enhance/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Enhance/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1enhance/get) Check an AI Photo Enhance task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/enhance

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/enhance

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of AI Photo Enhance task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/Al-Photo-Background-Removal](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/Al-Photo-Background-Removal) Al Photo Background Removal

### AI Photo Background Removal

Remove background from photo with impeccable accuracy, ensuring the high quality of images.

- Automatic Background Detection: : Uses AI to identify and separate the subject from the background.
- High Precision Editing: : Provides clean and precise edges around the subject.
- Supports various categories: People, Products, Animals, Cars, Graphics & more.
- Easy to chain with other AI tasks: The output file ID can be chained into other AI tasks in a flash.

Sample usage:
![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2023-11-03/54285311-7c65-4658-9e27-11bf5c8dfe56.jpg)

Sample uasge:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/Transparen_Background_aca3cdbd83.jpg)

Sample input:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_removal_bg_s4_poster_1_289b8eaf81.png)

Sample output:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_removal_bg_s4_poster_2_a6bc3c5f6a.png)

## [tag/AI-Photo-Colorize/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Colorize/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize/post) Run a AI Photo Colorize task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the file to run colorize. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Photo Colorize task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

## [tag/AI-Photo-Colorize/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Colorize/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize/get) Check a AI Photo Colorize task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of AI Photo Colorize task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of category and its styles

| |     |     |

| thumb<br>required | string<br>The thumbnail of style | | |

| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

| name<br>required | string<br>The name of sub-category. | | |

## [tag/AI-Image-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1text-to-image/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1text-to-image/post) Run a AI Image Generator task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/text-to-image

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/text-to-image

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| prompt<br>required | string<br>Prompt to generate image |
| negative\_prompt | string<br>Prompt what DO NOT want |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. |
| steps | integer<br>Steps affect image quality and time of processing |
| cfg\_scale | number<br>CFG controls how closely the generated image follows text prompt |
| seed | Array of integers<br>Each image is generated with a unique seed. Using same seed to recreate the same image. Only accept 1 seed. |
| width\_ratio | integer<br>The width of ratio of image. |
| height\_ratio | integer<br>The height of ratio of image. | | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Image Generator task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript

- Java

## [tag/AI-Image-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1text-to-image/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1text-to-image/get) Check a AI Image Generator task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/text-to-image

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/text-to-image

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of AI Image Generator task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Image-Extender](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-Extender) AI Image Extender

### AI Image Extender

Experience vibrant AI Outpainting with our cutting-edge AI Image Extender. Seamlessly expand images in any ratio, bringing out your creativity with our advanced AI technology. Preserve the highest quality while expanding your photos without compromising on style or aesthetics. Instantly transform your photos with one-click automatic background enlargement thanks to our user-friendly AI tool. Thanks to our advanced context-aware technology, we ensure a seamless and captivating experience for every viewer.

![AI Image Extender](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_web_outpainting_S1_img_03_cf19a018d9.jpg)

Whether you're aiming for Instagram glory or framing a digital masterpiece, select from a variety of sizes and ratios for that perfect fit. As you tweak and transform, our AI seamlessly weaves its magic, ensuring the expanded areas blend flawlessly with your original photo.

![AI Image Extender](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_web_outpainting_S1_img_01_1876fb85a5.jpg)

## [tag/AI-Image-Extender/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1out-paint/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-Extender/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1out-paint/post) Run an AI Image Extender task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/out-paint

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/out-paint

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to run enhancement. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object<br>The AI Image Extender API takes 3 key parameters to work, an input image, a pivot point and an output image. The size of output image should always be larger than the size of input image. And the recommeded size of output image should be less than two times of the size of input image to ensure better quality. The pivot point with location `input_x` and `input_y` is used to place the top-left of input image to the output image. You need to scale the input image by youself first if any of edges of the input image is larger than 4096. Or using the crop parameters to crop the input image. After cropping, you need to make sure the input image is completely inside the output image with your pivot point. It is your resposibility to provide correct pivot point and size of the output image. Otherwise, you may get unexpected results. |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| output\_width<br>required | integer<br>Output image height. value range: \[1 - 4096\] |
| output\_height<br>required | integer<br>Output image width. value range: \[1 - 4096\] |
| input\_x<br>required | integer<br>Source image left position in output image, where The indices are ordered from top to bottom, and from left to right. value range: \[0 - 4096\] |
| input\_y<br>required | integer<br>Source image top position in output image, where The indices are ordered from top to bottom, and from left to right. value range: \[0 - 4096\] |
| input\_width<br>required | integer<br>Source image width, input\_x + input\_width must ⇐ output\_width. value range: \[1 - 4096\] |
| input\_height<br>required | integer<br>Source image height, input\_y + input\_height must ⇐ output\_height. value range: \[1 - 4096\] |
| crop\_input\_x<br>required | integer<br>Crop source image from x, where The indices are ordered from top to bottom, and from left to right. value range: \[0 - 4096\] |
| crop\_input\_y<br>required | integer<br>Crop source image from y, where The indices are ordered from top to bottom, and from left to right. value range: \[0 - 4096\] |
| crop\_input\_width<br>required | integer<br>Crop source image with width crop\_input\_width. value range: \[1 - 4096\] |
| crop\_input\_height<br>required | integer<br>Crop source image with height crop\_input\_height. value range: \[1 - 4096\] | | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Image Extender task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

### Request samples
