## [tag/AI-Photo-Lighting/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1lighting/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Lighting/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1lighting/post) Run an AI Photo Lighting task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/lighting

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/lighting

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to run enhancement. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Photo Lighting task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

"payload": {

"src_ids": [\
"pfNK5PuRe0MrwLHcGA3DOmB1ahwfXTbYHjv+KoBIxbE="]},
"actions": [\
{\
"id": 0,\
"params": { }}]}}`

## [tag/AI-Photo-Lighting/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1lighting/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Lighting/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1lighting/get) Check an AI Photo Lighting task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/lighting

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/lighting

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

Successful check of AI Photo Lighting task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

### AI Color Correction

Perfect AI Color Correction let you automatically adjust saturation, temperature, and hue of photos with ease. Adjust white balance to correct color temperature, enhance saturation and make it vibrant, correct exposure level to balance brightness, remove color casts or tints, improve skin tones for a nature-looking portrait, enhance shadow and highlight details, remove noise and improve clarity, or even apply creative color grading effects all in one touch. With AI Color Correction, you can instantly generate 4 different color graded versions of your photos, each with unique color tones ranging from warm to cool within seconds.

## [tag/AI-Photo-Color-Correction/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize~1color-correct/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Color-Correction/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize~1color-correct/post) Run a AI Photo Color Correction task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize/color-correct

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize/color-correct

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the file to correct color. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Photo Color Correction task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript

- Python
- Java

"payload": {
"file_sets": {
"src_ids": [\
"pfNK5PuRe0MrwLHcGA3DOmB1ahwfXTbYHjv+KoBIxbE="]},
"actions": [\
{\
"id": 0}]}}`

## [tag/AI-Photo-Color-Correction/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize~1color-correct/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Color-Correction/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1colorize~1color-correct/get) Check a AI Photo Color Correction task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize/color-correct

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/colorize/color-correct

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of AI Photo Color Correction task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Replace](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Replace) AI Replace

### Al Replace

Replace unwanted elements with new objects using AI Replace. By using this API, you can instantly remove unwanted object from your photo and replace it with a new one just by using text. Eliminate anything from bags to cars and beyond.​

Sample:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_web_AI_replace_S3_feature_img_02_a73a26bcc3.jpg)

![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_web_AI_replace_S3_feature_img_03_42c9cd98d0.jpg)

## [tag/AI-Replace/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1obj-replace/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Replace/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1obj-replace/post) Run an AI Replace task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/obj-replace

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/obj-replace

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of main image. File ID from upload file API. |
| msk\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of masked area image. This should be a grey scale mask image with the exact same width and hight with the input image where white pixels indicate foregroud and black pixels represent background. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| prompt<br>required | string<br>Prompt for generating objects in the masked area. | | | |

## [tag/AI-Photo-Background-Change](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Background-Change) AI Photo Background Change

### AI Photo Background Change

The AI Photo Background Change tool enhances photos by effortlessly isolating the subject from the background image, allowing for various application, including in business, to sharpen the focus on product subjects.

By using this API, you can easily extract a foreground mask from a input image. So that you can change the background using the mask by any other images or colors.

Sample
Before:
![](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/assets/images/sod/banner/change/yce-topbanner-dt-before.jpg)

After:
![](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/assets/images/sod/banner/change/yce-topbanner-dt-after.jpg)

After:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_change_bg_s5_poster_after_7fb288fde2.jpg)

## [tag/AI-Photo-Background-Change/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1sod~1change-background/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Background-Change/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1sod~1change-background/post) Run an AI photo Background Change task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/sod/change-background

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/sod/change-background

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Repeated requests with the same request ID will be ignored by the server. This ID should remain consistent for retries due to connection issues. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the file to change background. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each actiond. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` s will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Photo Background Change task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- Payload
- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

Content type

application/json

Copy
Expand all  Collapse all

`{
"request_id": 0,
"payload": {
"file_sets": {
"src_ids": [\
"pfNK5PuRe0MrwLHcGA3DOmB1ahwfXTbYHjv+KoBIxbE="]},
"actions": [\
{\
"id": 0}]}}`

### Response samples

- 200
- 400
- 401

Content type

application/json

Copy
Expand all  Collapse all

`{
"status": 200,
"result": {
"task_id": "SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID"}}`

## [tag/AI-Photo-Background-Change/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1sod~1change-background/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Background-Change/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1sod~1change-background/get) Check AI photo Background Change task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/sod/change-background

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/sod/change-background

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of AI Photo Background Change task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

### Request samples

- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

```
curl --request GET \
    --url 'https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/sod/change-background?task_id=SX9ALF1Z%2BKIiNa%2BGaFRp4bI5gijoc%2FckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc%2B%2B3iXXdKqnU4%2FLID' \
    --header 'Authorization: Bearer <access_token>'
```

## [tag/AI-Photo-Background-Blur](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Photo-Background-Blur) AI Photo Background Blur

### AI Photo Background Blur

The AI Photo Background Blur tool enhances photos by effortlessly isolating the subject from the background image, allowing for various application, including in bokeh simulation, to sharpen the focus on product subjects.

By using this API, you can easily extract a foreground mask from a input image. So that you can blur the background using the mask by any image blur algorithms like the gaussian blur or custom blur kernels.

![](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/assets/images/sod/banner/blur/yce-topbanner-dt-before.jpg)

| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

| data | Array of objects |

## [tag/AI-Makeup-Transfer](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Makeup-Transfer) AI Makeup Transfer

### AI Makeup Transfer

Just Upload a Desired Photo with the Look You Like! AI Makeup Transfer makes it easy and fun to experiment with different looks by letting you to upload desired photo to try them one by one. Have any makeup look you want to try now? Let us amaze you with AI Makeup Transfer!

First, upload a photo of yourself where your face and its features are clearly visible as the target image.

Then, upload a photo of your favorite makeup look as the reference image.

There you have it - an AI Makeup Transferred photo.

Samples:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/YCE_web_Makeup_Transfer_s1_img_be53c5c345.jpg)

![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2024-06-24/fda62e5d-ba58-4ecf-838a-c7d5f804c77b.jpg)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Makeup Transfer | 1024x1024 (long side <= 1024), single face only, need to show full face | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg/png |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_src\_no\_face | No face detected in the user image |
| error\_ref\_no\_face | No face detected in the reference image |
| error\_src\_face\_too\_small | Face in the user image is too small |
| error\_ref\_face\_too\_small | Face in the reference image is too small |
| error\_src\_large\_face\_angle | Frontal face required in the user image |
| error\_ref\_large\_face\_angle | Frontal face required in the reference image |
| error\_src\_eye\_closed | Eye is closed in the user image |
| error\_ref\_eye\_closed | Eye is closed in the reference image |
| error\_src\_eye\_occluded | Eye is occluded in the user image |
| error\_ref\_eye\_occluded | Eye is occluded in the reference image |
| error\_src\_lip\_occluded | Lip is occluded in the user image |
| error\_ref\_lip\_occluded | Lip is occluded in the reference image |
| error\_inappropriate\_ref\_case01 | For both eyes, hair is too close to eye or skin region beside eyetail is not large enough in the reference image |
| error\_inappropriate\_ref\_case02 | For one eye, hair is too close to eye or skin region beside eyetail is not large enough in the reference image. The other one is not frontal enough in the reference image |

## [tag/AI-Makeup-Transfer/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1mu-transfer/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Makeup-Transfer/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1mu-transfer/post) Run a AI Makeup Transfer task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/mu-transfer

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/mu-transfer

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the target image to transfer. File ID from upload file API. |
| ref\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the reference image. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Makeup Transfer task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/file/face-swap

To upload a new file, you'll first need to use the File API. It will give you a URL – use that URL to upload your file. Once the upload is finished, you can use the file\_id from the same response to start using our AI features.

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| files<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| content\_type<br>required | string<br>Enum:"image/jpg""image/jpeg""image/png"<br>Content MIME type for this file. Currently available values are listed in the enum. |
| file\_name<br>required | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_size<br>required | integer<br>Content length for this file in bytes. Should not be larger than 10MB. | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of file upload information

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| files | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| content\_type | string<br>Content MIME type for this file. |
| file\_name | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_id | string<br>ID of this file. Other run task API will need this `file_id`. |
| requests | Array of objects<br>Using upload `url`, `headers`, `method` below to upload file. After completion, the `file_id` is used to proceed with calling run task API. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

## [tag/AI-Face-Swap/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap~1pre-process/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Face-Swap/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap~1pre-process/post) Run a AI Face Swap face detection task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap/pre-process

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap/pre-process

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the target image to detect face. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Face Swap face detection task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

## [tag/AI-Face-Swap/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap~1pre-process/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Face-Swap/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap~1pre-process/get) Check a AI Face Swap face detection task status

get/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap/pre-process

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap/pre-process

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of AI Face Swap face detection task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours |
| faces | Array of objects | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Face-Swap/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Face-Swap/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap/post) Run a AI Face Swap task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the target image for swap. |
| ref\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the reference image. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| face\_mapping<br>required | Array of objects<br>The designated ref image id and face position information to be swapped for each detected face on target image.<br>e.g. \[{'index': 0, 'position': 1}\] indicates that the second face on the target image is going to be swapped with the first reference image |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| index | integer<br>The index of reference image |
| position | integer<br>The index of face on the target image. The index is from faces of detection result. | | | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of AI Face Swap task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

Failed execution of task

## [tag/AI-Headshot-Generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Headshot-Generator) AI Headshot Generator

### AI Headshot Generator

Transform your photos into stunning professional deadshots with our AI Headshot Generator. Elevate your headshots quickly and effectively using our powerful AI tools designed to deliver professional-quality results.

- Variety of Styles: From polished LinkedIn headshots and professional business headshots to creative model headshots, our AI headshot generator helps you select the perfect look to suit your needs.
- Professional Results: Leveraging AI to ensure your headshots look natural and flattering, making a strong impression on potential employers and clients.
- Convenience: Generate multiple AI headshots anytime, anywhere, without the need for a photographer. Perfect for busy professionals.

For more AI Headshot styles, please refer to [https://yce.perfectcorp.com/ai-headshot-generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/ai-headshot-generator).

Use cases:
![AI Headshot Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_headshot_s2_img_03_4b55742358.jpg)

![AI Headshot Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_headshot_s1_img_1_d03183d7e0.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Headshot | Ensure the input image contains a single person with both shoulder points and a full face visible from OpenPose, and that its short side is ≤ 1024 pixels—otherwise, the engine will automatically resize it to 1024. Output: long side <= 1024 | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg |

##### Authorizations:

| file\_name<br>required | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_size<br>required | integer<br>Content length for this file in bytes. Should not be larger than 10MB. | |

### Responses

Successful retrieval of file upload information

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| files | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| content\_type | string<br>Content MIME type for this file. |
| file\_name | string<br>Name of this file |
| file\_id | string<br>ID of this file. Other run task API will need this `file_id`. |
| requests | Array of objects<br>Using upload `url`, `headers`, `method` below to upload file. After completion, the `file_id` is used to proceed with calling run task API. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| headers | object<br>Headers to include when uploading the file |
| url | string<br>URL to upload this file |
| method | string<br>HTTP method to upload this file | | | |

**400**

Invalid request parameters

**401**

## [tag/AI-Headshot-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1headshot/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Headshot-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1headshot/get) List predefined style by category

get/s2s/v1.1/task/style/headshot

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/headshot

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of category and its styles

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| results | Array of objects (Category) |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of category. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of category. |
| styles<br>required | Array of objects (Style) <br>The styles belong to this category. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style group. Use this as `style_group_id` when run task. |
| style\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style. Use this as `style_ids` when run task. |
| info<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| title<br>required | string<br>The style name |
| thumb<br>required | string<br>The thumbnail of style | | |
| sub\_categories<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of sub-category. Use this id to query for its content. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of sub-category. | | |

## [tag/AI-Headshot-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1headshot/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Headshot-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1headshot/post) Run an AI Headshot Generator task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/headshot

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/headshot

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. The number of styles must be less than or equal to the output\_count. | | |
| custom<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| output\_count<br>required | integer \[ 1 .. 200 \] <br>The number of generated images. It must be between 1 to 200. | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Headshot Generator task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- curl
- Node.js

"id": 0,\

"custom": {
"output_count": 20},

## [tag/AI-Headshot-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1headshot/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Headshot-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1headshot/get) Check the status of the AI Headshot Generator task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/headshot

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/headshot

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Headshot Generator task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Avatar-Generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Avatar-Generator) AI Avatar Generator

### AI Avatar Generator

For the AI magic avatar tool, this app uses the technology of image-to-image. which means the avatar is generated based on your photo. Once the photos are selected by the users, the technology embedded in the app starts analyzing and learning the user's facial traits.

For more avatar styles, please refer to [https://yce.perfectcorp.com/avatar](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/avatar)

Use cases:
![AI Avatar Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/Christmas_Avatar_b861c35edf.jpg)

![AI Avatar Generator](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2023-04-06/fc2c3b2e-2b7f-48c9-96c1-cdb780f9dc1d.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

| page\_size | integer<br>Example: page\_size=20<br>Number of results to return in this page. Valid value should be between 1 and 20. Default 20. |

## [tag/AI-Avatar-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1ai-avatar/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Avatar-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1ai-avatar/get) List predefined style by category

get/s2s/v1.1/task/style/ai-avatar

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/ai-avatar

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of category and its styles

| name<br>required | string<br>The name of category. |
| styles<br>required | Array of objects (Style) <br>The styles belong to this category. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style group. Use this as `style_group_id` when run task. |
| style\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style. Use this as `style_ids` when run task. |

| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| title<br>required | string<br>The style name |
| thumb<br>required | string<br>The thumbnail of style | | |
| sub\_categories<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of sub-category. Use this id to query for its content. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of sub-category. | | |

## [tag/AI-Avatar-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-avatar/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Avatar-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-avatar/post) Run an AI Avatar task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-avatar

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-avatar

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. The number of styles must be less than or equal to the output\_count. | | |
| custom<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| output\_count<br>required | integer \[ 1 .. 200 \] <br>The number of generated images. It must be between 1 to 200. | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Avatar task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

"output_count": 20},

"string"]}}}`

## [tag/AI-Avatar-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-avatar/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Avatar-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-avatar/get) Check the status of the AI Avatar task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-avatar

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-avatar

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Avatar task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Studio-Generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Studio-Generator) AI Studio Generator

### AI Studio Generator

Embrace the excellence of studio kike AI Portrait Generator. Transform your selfie into a studio-quality portrait in a flash​.

- Studio-Free Convenience: No need for a photographer or studio visits—create studio-quality artistic photos anytime, anywhere​
- Quick Photo Transformation: Fast processing for instant high-quality artistic photo results, ideal for quick updates
- High-Quality Artistic Output: Delivers professional-standard artistic photos with clear details, perfect lighting, just like you've taken the photos in a studio

Use cases:
![AI Studio Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_web_AI_studio_S1_img_19b627b6af.jpg)

![AI Studio Generator](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/yce_web_AI_studio_S2_img_01_2e318817e9.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![Suggestions for How to Shoot](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AI Studio | Please ensure the input image has one face, a short side of at least 200 pixels, and a long side no greater than 1920 pixels; the engine will select the largest face if multiple are present, and the output resolution will not exceed 960×1280 (W×H) | < 10MB | jpg/jpeg/png |

### Error Codes

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| error\_below\_min\_image\_size | Input image resolution is too small |
| error\_exceed\_max\_image\_size | Input image resolution is too large |

| page\_size | integer<br>Example: page\_size=20<br>Number of results to return in this page. Valid value should be between 1 and 20. Default 20. |

| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Example: style\_group\_id=18213963761051864<br>The id of style group |

## [tag/AI-Studio-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1ai-studio/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Studio-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1ai-studio/get) List predefined style by category

get/s2s/v1.1/task/style/ai-studio

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/ai-studio

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

Successful retrieval of category and its styles

| styles<br>required | Array of objects (Style) <br>The styles belong to this category. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style group. Use this as `style_group_id` when run task. |
| style\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style. Use this as `style_ids` when run task. |

| |     |     |
| --- | --- |

| Array

|     |     |

| name<br>required | string<br>The name of sub-category. | | |

## [tag/AI-Studio-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-studio/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Studio-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-studio/post) Run an AI Studio task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-studio

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-studio

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. The number of styles must be less than or equal to the output\_count. | | |
| custom<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| output\_count<br>required | integer \[ 1 .. 200 \] <br>The number of generated images. It must be between 1 to 200. | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Studio task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

### Request samples

- Payload
- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

{\
"id": 0,\
"params": {\
"style_group_id": 18213963761051864,\
"style_ids": [\

"custom": {
"output_count": 20},

"string"]}}}`

## [tag/AI-Studio-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-studio/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Studio-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1ai-studio/get) Check the status of the AI Studio task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-studio

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/ai-studio

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Studio task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

## [tag/AI-Image-to-Video-Generator](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-to-Video-Generator) AI Image to Video Generator

### AI Image to Video Generator

YouCam AI Image to Video Generator quickly turns one image into stunning videos using advanced algorithms to create realistic motion effects. Offers a variety of highly optimized pre-made templates to animate your photos.

To easily create a video from an image using AI, start with a photo that has a clean background and a clear portrait. Simply upload your photo, and watch the magic happen!

Use cases:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/strapi/assets/webp_Animate%20Photo_047_d9e1cff579.jpg)

![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Dance_Video_61cf4c58d1.png)

![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/241216_AI_Kiss_image05_c3b7f1ac5b.jpg)

Suggestions for How to Shoot:
![](https://bcw-media.s3.ap-northeast-1.amazonaws.com/AI_Hair_Extension_recommendation_ba24bd5d92.png)

### Supported Formats & Dimensions

| AI Feature | Supported Dimensions | Supported File Size | Supported Formats |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Image to Video (Standard) | Input: >= 300\*300px with aspect ratio between 1:2.5 ~ 2.5:1. Output: Up to 720p 30fps | Input: <10MB. Output: 5 seconds or 10 seconds | jpg/jpeg/png |
| Image to Video (Professional) | Input: >= 300\*300px with aspect ratio between 1:2.5 ~ 2.5:1. Output: Up to 1080p 30fps | Input: <10MB. Output: 5 seconds or 10 seconds | jpg/jpeg/png |

### Error Codes

| Error Message | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Invalid request parameters | Check whether the request parameters are correct |
| Invalid parameters, such as incorrect key or illegal value | Refer to the specific information in the message field of the returned body and modify the request parameters |
| The requested method is invalid | Review the API documentation and use the correct request method |
| The requested resource does not exist, such as the model | Refer to the specific information in the message field of the returned body and modify the request parameters |
| Trigger strategy of the platform | Check if any platform policies have been triggered |
| Trigger the content security policy of the platform | Check the input content, modify it, and resend the request |
| Server internal error | Try again later, or contact customer service |
| Server temporarily unavailable, usually due to maintenance | Try again later, or contact customer service |
| Server internal timeout, usually due to a backlog | Try again later, or contact customer service |

There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. ## [tag/AI-Image-to-Video-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1image-to-video/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-to-Video-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1image-to-video/post) Run an Image to Video task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/image-to-video

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/image-to-video

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. |
| mode | string<br>Enum:"std""pro"<br>The quailty mode. Standard (std) mode is faster speed, OK quailty. Professional (pro) mode is best quailty with richer details. Automatically select best mode by style if not provide. | | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API | |
| custom<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_duration<br>required | integer<br>The length of video in seconds. Only accept 5 or 10 seconds | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the Image to Video task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

## [tag/AI-Image-to-Video-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1image-to-video/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Image-to-Video-Generator/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1image-to-video/get) Check the status of the Image to Video task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/image-to-video

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/image-to-video

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

Successful check of the Image to Video task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

### AI Video Enhance

Fix blur, adjust sharpness and brightness, and instantly transform low-quality videos into clear, high-quality content with AI. From 480p to 4K, unblur, upscale, and boost quality with the video enhancer—no skills needed.

Supported format: .mp4, .mov are supported. Please keep the duration under 1 minute.
Maximun output resolution: up to 4K.

This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |

| custom | object |
| |     |     |

## [tag/AI-Face-Swap-(video)](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Face-Swap-(video)) AI Face Swap (video)

### AI Video Face Swap

Video face swapping is an AI-powered process that uses YouCam’s AI Video Face Swap API to replace one person's face with another in a video.
With advanced AI technology, the AI video face swap delivers remarkably realistic results. The facial expressions, lighting, and skin tones are finely tuned to ensure that the swapped faces blend seamlessly with the original footage.

> **Note:** This API supports video with single face only. For customizable solution, please [contact us](mailto:YouCamOnlineEditor_API@perfectcorp.com).

Sample usage cases:
![](https://plugins-media.makeupar.com/smb/blog/post/2024-08-23/b1f96100-37d6-4c28-b467-d397e9c3a25d.jpg)
