## [tag/AI-Face-Swap-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap-vid/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Face-Swap-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap-vid/post) Run an AI Face Swap (video) task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap-vid

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap-vid

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the target video for swap. |
| ref\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of the reference image. File ID from upload file API. | |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. | |
| custom<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_duration<br>required | integer<br>The length of video in seconds | | |

### Request samples

- Payload
- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

Content type

application/json

Copy
Expand all  Collapse all

`{
"request_id": 0,
"payload": {
"file_sets": {
"src_ids": [\
"pfNK5PuRe0MrwLHcGA3DOmB1ahwfXTbYHjv+KoBIxbE="],
"ref_ids": [\
"ligsPdfZTgNrbXnAOsPMFCiKyqGEJWl7SkYBBv6mHUac8ywz/bnMOrhVtlbo86Mc"]},
"actions": [\
{\
"id": 0}],
"custom": {
"dst_duration": 0}}}`

## [tag/AI-Face-Swap-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap-vid/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Face-Swap-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1face-swap-vid/get) Check the status of the AI Face Swap (video) task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap-vid

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap-vid

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Face Swap (video) task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

### Request samples

- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

Copy

```
curl --request GET \
    --url 'https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/face-swap-vid?task_id=SX9ALF1Z%2BKIiNa%2BGaFRp4bI5gijoc%2FckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc%2B%2B3iXXdKqnU4%2FLID' \
    --header 'Authorization: Bearer <access_token>'
```

### Response samples

- 200
- 400
- 401
- 500

Content type

application/json

Copy
Expand all  Collapse all

`{
"status": 200,
"result": {
"polling_interval": 1000,
"status": "running",
"error": "exceed_max_filesize",
"error_message": "string",
"results": [\
{\
"id": 0,\
"data": [\
{\
"dst_id": "Iq4cbOV90rXJHSTfBGBTTYXBF9p1B0xCmy8nIrjTa10=",\
"url": "https://s3-us-west-2.amazonaws.com/yce-us/gst_tsk/a29e54f4-03a8-4ff1-9226-d6c83ae86053/34516942129/cf4d1764-4517-44af-aed8-fc78fc186072.jpg?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Date=20240101T120225Z&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&X-Amz-Expires=7200&X-Amz-Credential=AKIARB77EV5YXEKPIQMM%2F20240101%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Signature=f199a5da82b0b171d873098ab91473f57a872e3b6cfa58ff6ca24e48617fabc0"}]}]}}`

## [tag/AI-Style-Transfer-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1video-trans/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Style-Transfer-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.1~1task~1style~1video-trans/get) List predefined style by category

get/s2s/v1.1/task/style/video-trans

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/video-trans

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| category\_id | Array of integers <= 5 items <br>The id of category. Accepts multiple values, up to a maximum of 5. There are two ways to list styles for AI task: - v1.0: Retrieve style groups first, then fetch styles within the chosen group. - v1.1: Fetch a predefined style list by category. If you don’t specify a category\_id, each category will contain either styles or subcategories. Categories with a single layer only include styles, while multi-layered categories will have subcategories. To explore a subcategory, pass its ID as category\_id and call the list again. |

### Responses

**200**

Successful retrieval of category and its styles

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| results | Array of objects (Category) |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of category. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of category. |
| styles<br>required | Array of objects (Style) <br>The styles belong to this category. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style group. Use this as `style_group_id` when run task. |
| style\_id<br>required | integer<br>The id of style. Use this as `style_ids` when run task. |
| info<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| title<br>required | string<br>The style name |
| thumb<br>required | string<br>The thumbnail of style | | |
| sub\_categories<br>required | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>The id of sub-category. Use this id to query for its content. |
| name<br>required | string<br>The name of sub-category. | | |

**400**

Invalid request parameters

### Request samples

- Node.js

```

    --url 'https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.1/task/style/video-trans?category_id=SOME_ARRAY_VALUE' \
    --header 'Authorization: Bearer <access_token>'
```

## [tag/AI-Style-Transfer-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1video-trans/post](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Style-Transfer-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1video-trans/post) Run an AI Style Transfer (video) task

post/s2s/v1.0/task/video-trans

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/video-trans

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### Request Body schema: application/json  required

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| request\_id<br>required | integer<br>Incremental request number starting from 0. Requests with the same `request_id` will be ignored by the server. `request_id` should remain the same if the API client needs to retry the API due to a connection issue. This is to prevent duplicate deduction of units caused by running the same task repeatedly. For instance, if the same `file_id` is sent with the same `request_id`, the engine won't re-run the task, nor will duplicate consume units. However, if a client wants to generate multiple different results using the same `file_id`, the client needs to increment the `request_id` then the engine will re-run the task and consume the unit accordingly. |
| payload<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| actions<br>required | Array of objects<br>Only accept 1 action. |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id<br>required | integer<br>ID of this action, start with 0. The client needs to generate an `id` for each action. This action `id` has to be unique per task. In the response from the get status API, these action `id` will be used to let the client know which results correspond to each action. |
| params<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| style\_group\_id<br>required | integer<br>Id of style group |
| style\_ids<br>required | Array of numbers<br>Id of style to run the task. Only accept 1 style. | | |
| file\_sets<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| src\_ids<br>required | Array of strings<br>ID of file to apply task. File ID from upload file API | |
| custom<br>required | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_duration<br>required | integer<br>The length of video in seconds | | |

### Responses

**200**

Successful execution of the AI Style Transfer (video) task

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id | string<br>ID of this task. This `task_id` will only valid if client continue polling check status API with interval `polling_interval` defined in check status API response. Otherwise, engine might consider client have leave and will not process the task. No unit will be consumed in this case. | |

**400**

Failed execution of task

**401**

Invalid access token

**429**

Too many requests within a given amount of time

## [tag/AI-Style-Transfer-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1video-trans/get](https://yce.perfectcorp.com/document/index.html\#tag/AI-Style-Transfer-(video)/paths/~1s2s~1v1.0~1task~1video-trans/get) Check the status of the AI Style Transfer (video) task

get/s2s/v1.0/task/video-trans

https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/video-trans

##### Authorizations:

_BearerAuthentication_

##### query Parameters

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| task\_id<br>required | string<br>Example: task\_id=SX9ALF1Z+KIiNa+GaFRp4bI5gijoc/ckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc++3iXXdKqnU4/LID<br>ID of task to check |

### Responses

**200**

Successful check of the AI Style Transfer (video) task status

##### Response Schema: application/json

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| status | integer<br>Response status |
| result | object |
| |     |     |
| --- | --- |
| polling\_interval | integer<br>Milliseconds waiting time for start next polling. Note that the task will lose if no polling in 10 seconds |
| status | string<br>Enum:"running""success""error"<br>Status of this task |
| error | string or null (EngineErrorCode) <br>Enum:"exceed\_max\_filesize""invalid\_parameter""error\_download\_image""error\_download\_mask""error\_decode\_image""error\_decode\_mask""error\_nsfw\_content\_detected""error\_no\_face""error\_pose""error\_face\_parsing""error\_inference""exceed\_nsfw\_retry\_limits""error\_upload""unknown\_internal\_error"<br>Errors:<br>- `exceed_max_filesize` \- Input file size exceeds the maximum limit<br>- `invalid_parameter` \- Invalid parameter value<br>- `error_download_image` \- Download source image error<br>- `error_download_mask` \- Download mask image error<br>- `error_decode_image` \- Decode source image error<br>- `error_decode_mask` \- Decode mask image error<br>- `error_nsfw_content_detected` \- NSFW content detected in source image<br>- `error_no_face` \- No face detected on source image<br>- `error_pose` \- Failed to detect pose on source image<br>- `error_face_parsing` \- Failed to do face segmentation on source image<br>- `error_inference` \- Inference pipeline error<br>- `exceed_nsfw_retry_limits` \- Exceed the retry limits to avoid generated NSFW image<br>- `error_upload` \- Upload result image error<br>- `unknown_internal_error` \- Others |
| error\_message | string<br>Detailed description of error |
| results | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| id | integer<br>ID of action |
| data | Array of objects |
| Array

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| dst\_id | string<br>File ID of the result file is used for integrating other task. No need to reupload file. |
| url | string<br>URL to download this result. Valid for 2 hours | | | |

**400**

Invalid task id

**401**

Invalid access token

**500**

The task has no response in the expected time

### Request samples

- curl
- Node.js
- JavaScript
- PHP
- Python
- Java

```
    --url 'https://yce-api-01.perfectcorp.com/s2s/v1.0/task/video-trans?task_id=SX9ALF1Z%2BKIiNa%2BGaFRp4bI5gijoc%2FckI2teebLq35Bo1Nwc%2B%2B3iXXdKqnU4%2FLID' \
    --header 'Authorization: Bearer <access_token>'
```
